  <span m='5087480'>that</span> <span m='5087700'>you</span> <span m='5087890'>do</span>

  <span m='5090770'>you</span> <span m='5090930'>have</span> <span m='5091210'>to</span>
  <span m='5091330'>get</span> <span m='5091670'>back</span> <span m='5091980'>up</span>
  <span m='5092200'>to</span> <span m='5092350'>where</span> <span m='5092745'>a sign</span>
  <span m='5093140'>actually</span> <span m='5093840'>disappears</span> <span m='5094530'>to</span>
  <span m='5094650'>where</span> <span m='5094850'>you</span> <span m='5095040'>want.</span>
  <span m='5095800'>You</span> <span m='5096540'>have</span> <span m='5096790'>to</span>
  <span m='5096910'>multiply</span> <span m='5097610'>by</span> <span m='5097780'>two</span>
  <span m='5098000'>Jacobians,</span> <span m='5098820'>and</span> <span m='5098940'>you</span>
  <span m='5099060'>get</span> <span m='5099750'>the</span> <span m='5099860'>same</span>
  <span m='5100360'>unit.</span> <span m='5101560'>You</span> <span m='5101670'>can</span>
  <span m='5101880'>convince</span> <span m='5102390'>yourself</span> <span m='5102880'>that</span>
  <span m='5103050'>this</span> <span m='5103240'>Jacobian</span> <span m='5103850'>has</span>
  <span m='5104100'>to</span> <span m='5104190'>be</span> <span m='5104640'>unit.</span>
  </p><p><span m='5105730'>Next</span> <span m='5106130'>time,</span> <span m='5106390'>I</span>
  <span m='5106500'>guess</span> <span m='5106760'>we'll</span> <span m='5106960'>take</span>
  <span m='5107390'>it</span> <span m='5107560'>from</span> <span m='5107860'>there.</span>
  <span m='5108340'>I will</span> <span m='5108700'>explain</span> <span m='5109330'>this</span>
  <span m='5109630'>stuff</span> <span m='5109840'>a</span> <span m='5109890'>little</span>
  <span m='5110220'>bit</span> <span m='5110470'>more,</span> <span m='5111180'>and</span>
  <span m='5111505'>show</span> <span m='5111830'>that</span> <span m='5112080'>this</span>
  <span m='5113040'>implies</span> <span m='5114140'>what</span> <span m='5114320'>we</span>
  <span m='5114490'>had</span> <span m='5114710'>said</span> <span m='5114960'>about</span>
